<![CDATA[ <p>Myticas's direct client is seeking <em><strong>Scrum Master (AI Enablement team) - </strong></em><strong>Hypid</strong> at Waukegan, IL (3 days Onsite / 2 Remote).</p> <p><strong>Duration:</strong> 1 Year Contract (Potential of Extension)</p> <p><strong><u>TOP 5 Skills/Experience:</u></strong></p> <ol> <li>7-10 years of experience as Project Manager / ScrumMaster <li><strong>Experience working with AI in Day-to-Day Work: Leverage AI (Artificial Intelligence) tools to drive innovation, efficiency and decision making.</strong> <li>Expertise of <strong>Agile Facilitation and Scrum Methodologies</strong> <li>Expertise in Jira <li>SharePoint Expertise for Enhanced Collaboration <li>Skilled in Storytelling and Developing Training and Communication Materials </ol> <p><strong>Job Summary</strong></p> <ul> <li>As a Scrum Master within our AI Enablement organization, you will play a crucial role in facilitating agile teams focused on advancing AI initiatives across the enterprise, with a strong emphasis on enhancing AI learning and education. <li>Your responsibilities will include fostering collaboration and driving continuous improvement, while effectively addressing obstacles to ensure the timely and high-quality delivery of AI capabilities and learning solutions. <li>Collaboration is paramount, and you will work cross-functionally with diverse professionals including developers, business stakeholders, technical experts, and leadership to ensure the seamless integration of agile practices. <li>Your pivotal role will champion AI learning, supporting the cultivation of an AI-proficient workforce that can meet future challenges. </ul> <p><strong>Required Experience:</strong></p> <ul> <li>7-10 years of experience as Project Manager / ScrumMaster <li>Mastery of Agile Facilitation and Scrum Methodologies: Guide agile teams to enhance productivity and innovation in delivering impactful AI initiatives. This involves applying Scrum principles to manage workload efficiently. <li>Demonstrated Experience Working with AI in Day-to-Day Work: Leverage AI tools to drive innovation, efficiency and decision making. <li>Expertise in Jira: Use Jira for tracking project progress, managing backlogs and reporting on key project metrics. <li>Strong Organizational and Communication Skills: Maintain effective communication with the team and stakeholders. <li>Facilitate structured organization and time management to handle multiple projects and commitments efficiently. <li>Leading Change Management: lead change management efforts that drive the adoption of AI-driven capabilities organization-wide. <li>SharePoint Expertise for Enhanced Collaboration: Utilize your SharePoint skills to refine site content and design, fostering seamless collaboration and optimal resource management. <li>Skilled in Storytelling and Developing Training and Communication Materials: Harness storytelling to create engaging narratives. Develop compelling, high-quality training and communication materials to ensure effective program delivery. </ul> <p><em><strong>PMP Certification is preferred.</strong></em></p> ]]>

practices, testing, and documentation.</p> <li> <p>Optimize site performance through Search API integrations with ElasticSearch.</p> <li> <p>Lead or support complex Drupal migrations using the <strong>Drupal Migrate</strong> module.</p> <li> <p>Apply and create patches to core and contrib modules as necessary.</p> <li> <p>Integrate and develop web services (RESTful APIs) and support external integrations.</p> <li> <p>Collaborate with front-end developers using JavaScript and CSS/Sass to create seamless user experiences.</p> <li> <p>Utilize container-based development environments using <strong>Docker DDEV</strong> or work in <strong>VirtualBox</strong>-based systems (e.g., AlmaLinux).</p> <li> <p>Manage source control, branching, and CI/CD pipelines using <strong>Git</strong> and <strong>GitHub Actions</strong>.</p> <li> <p>Participate in code reviews, sprint planning, and DevOps discussions.</p> </ul> <p><strong>Required Qualifications:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>5+ years <![CDATA[ <p><strong>Job Title: Senior Identity and Access Management (IAM) Consultant – Oracle 12C OIM Data Migration</strong></p> <p><strong>Background:</strong></p> <p>Ontario Health’s <strong>ONE ID</strong> service is a secure identity management solution utilized by the Ministry of Health and Long-Term Care, as well as numerous healthcare organizations across Ontario. It enables secure access to patient health information (PHI) through a single set of login credentials while upholding stringent privacy and security standards.</p> <p>The ONE ID platform is based on the Oracle Identity and Access Management suite, including Oracle Access Manager (OAM), Oracle Unified Directory (OUD), Oracle Identity Manager (OIM), Oracle Database, Microsoft Active Directory (AD), and custom Ontario Health systems.</p> <p>Ontario Health is undertaking an upgrade to Oracle 12C IAM and requires the services of a <strong>Senior Identity and Access Management Consultant</strong> to support the data migration and integration activities necessary to transition from Oracle 10G/11G to 12C. The consultant will be embedded within a dedicated project team responsible for the 12C Oracle IAM upgrade.</p> <hr> <h3><strong>Must-Have Qualifications:</strong></h3> <ul> <li> <p>Minimum 7 years of experience as a Solution Architect on Oracle Identity and Access Management systems (10G, 11G, 12C).</p> <li> <p>Minimum 7 years of experience with 12C Oracle Identity Governance (OIG), including successful migration of user, service enrollment, and organizational data from 10G to 12C.</p> <li> <p>Minimum 5 years of experience configuring 11G OIM and 12C OIG in a multi-data center (MDC) environment.</p> <li> <p>Minimum 7 years of experience integrating Oracle IAM suite components: OAM, OIM, OUD/OVD, Oracle HTTP Server (OHS), Microsoft Active Directory, and Oracle databases.</p> <li> <p>Minimum 5 years of experience tuning Oracle IAM for high availability on WebLogic and Linux platforms.</p> <li> <p>Experience designing and creating services and applications for enrollment in 12C OIG using native interfaces.</p> <li> <p>Experience configuring connectors and disconnected resources for service/application enrollment in 12C OIG.</p> <li> <p>Must be associated with a recognized Gold Oracle IAM Partner.</p> <li> <p>Expertise in SAML 2.0 and OAuth 2.0 protocols.</p> <li> <p>Proven ability to translate conceptual, logical, and physical application architectures aligned to business and technical goals.</p> <li> <p>Strong written and verbal communication skills with the ability to clearly articulate technical issues and propose viable solutions.</p> <li> <p>Ability to produce comprehensive technical documentation including design, deployment, and integration guides.</p> </ul> <hr> <h3><strong>Responsibilities:</strong></h3> <ul> <li> <p>Collaborate with Ontario Health teams to design and configure 12C OIG in a multi-data center setup for both lower and upper environments.</p> <li> <p>Integrate Phase 1 of 12C MDC with the existing 10G ONE ID system to enable interoperability for user and service transition.</p> <li> <p>Create and maintain service/application enrollments in 12C OIG.</p> <li> <p>Develop enrollment flows for individual services/applications.</p> <li> <p>Document design, installation, configuration, and integration procedures across all environments.</p> <li> <p>Collaborate with the Applications and Architecture teams to resolve cross-domain and technical issues related to the 12C implementation (e.g., return URL configuration).</p> <li> <p>Work closely with database, networking, and infrastructure teams at Ontario Health.</p> <li> <p>Provide weekly progress updates to team leads and the project manager.</p> </ul> <hr> <h3><strong>Desired Skills:</strong></h3> <ul> <li> <p>Experience with the Oracle IAM Suite Plus and Microsoft Active Directory Suite.</p> <li> <p>In-depth knowledge of IAM best practices.</p> <li> <p>Experience integrating business applications with Oracle IAM and Microsoft AD.</p> <li> <p>Strong troubleshooting skills for diagnosing and resolving IAM-related issues.</p> <li> <p>Experience with service and user identity development in OIM and OIG.</p> <li> <p>Understanding of IT security concepts, especially PKI, encryption, TLS/SSL.</p> <li> <p>Proficiency in Agile development methodologies and Continuous Integration/Continuous Deployment (CI/CD).</p> <li> <p>Familiarity with JIRA and Confluence.</p> <li> <p>Ability to collaborate with:</p> <ul> <li> <p>Internal and external stakeholders to assess integration needs.</p> <li> <p>Architects and policy/security teams across domains.</p> <li> <p>Solution vendors and development teams to ensure architectural compliance.</p> <li> <p>External organizations (e.g., Ministry of Health, Canada Health Infoway) to ensure alignment.</p> </ul> </ul> ]]>

<description>
<![CDATA[ <p><strong>Overview & Role Focus</strong></p> <p>This role is centered on innovating and advancing state-of-the-art video processing and transport capabilities, delivering high-performance solutions on some of the most integrated poadcast hardware platforms available today. The successful candidate will work hands-on with FPGA design, real-time media interfaces, and poadcast protocol implementation, playing a key role across architecture, development, testing, and cross-functional support.</p> <p><strong>Key Responsibilities</strong></p> <ul> <li>Lead the development and continuous improvement of advanced video transport and processing features within tightly integrated poadcast hardware. <li>Design RTL for real-time, high-throughput media systems involving advanced interfaces—such as PCIe, memory, and specialized hardware acceleration (e.g., video scaling, HDR/SDR conversion). <li>Implement FPGA-based real-time transport protocols like SMPTE 2110 and SDI. <li>Participate in architectural planning: advise on FPGA density, schematic reviews, clocking strategies, and thermal considerations. <li>Build complete IO ring designs across modern FPGAs (Arria10, Stratix-10, Ultrascale+, MPSoC, Agilex) and validate pin-outs/IP within Quartus and Vivado environments. <li>Define and negotiate high-level design specs, assist in part selection, and align with aggressive project timelines. <li>Contribute to design specifications and documentation used by cross-functional teams. <li>Collaborate closely with peers on design verification and testing of FPGA and hardware systems. <li>Tackle debugging with a methodical and efficient approach. <li>Support team members throughout the entire New Product Introduction (NPI) lifecycle—from design through manufacturing to customer support. </ul> <p><strong>Required Skills & Background</strong></p> <ul> <li>5+ years in FPGA and hardware development, with a strong preference for experience in video/audio-centric technologies. <li>Intermediate to senior-level expertise in FPGA architecture and core components. <li>Deep understanding of high-speed serial interfaces, clock domains, timing closure, and transceiver integration. <li>Proficiency in Verilog, SystemVerilog, and TCL scripting; capable of creating testbenches and running simulations (e.g., VCS). <li>Familiarity with modern Intel and Xilinx FPGA families and their development/debugging toolchains. <li>Hands-on experience with interfaces like DDR3/DDR4, HBM, PLLs, and gigabit transceivers. <li>Skilled in lab-based debugging using oscilloscopes, JBERTs, network analyzers, waveform monitors, etc. <li>Embedded system awareness—experience with Linux, C/C++, bash scripting, and networking considered valuable. <li>Broadcast studio domain knowledge is highly desirable, especially within video production and distribution workflows. <li>A strong grasp of digital video/audio standards and signal integrity is considered a plus. <li>Driven and independent, yet collaborative—equally adept at working solo or influencing poader team strategies. <li>Quick learner with a creative mindset and ability to push ideas from concept to market. <li>Comfortable making bold decisions that balance quality, speed, and cost for optimal business outcomes. <li>Effective communicator with sharp observational skills and a problem-solving mindset. </ul> ]]>
</description>

<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>As the Senior Manager of Radio System Engineering, you will lead all technical aspects of radio system architecture, including air interface definition, concept of operations, functional specifications, and physical implementation of RF functions.</p> <hr> <p><strong>Main Responsibilities:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Provide expert-level leadership in RF system development, including trade-offs involving ACP, PAR, out-of-band emissions, pass-band ripple, group delay, and more.</p> <li> <p>Support the finalization of radio system implementation involving agile multi-beam phased array antennas and beam hopping technology.</p> <li> <p>Define operational concepts for all phases of the system lifecycle such as user terminal commissioning, network entry, satellite handovers, time synchronization, and adaptive coding and modulation (ACM).</p> <li> <p>Act as the principal architect for defining air interfaces between user terminals, ground infrastructure, and satellite payloads.</p> <li> <p>Collaborate with RF, antenna, system, and terminal engineers to partition functionality between hardware and software components.</p> <li> <p>Provide input to the system modeling team on design assumptions and strategies for modeling link performance, accounting for impairments across system components.</p> <li> <p>Work closely with the Verification and Test team to ensure thorough validation of requirements and system performance.</p> <li> <p>Participate in relevant industry standards forums (e.g., DVB) and provide strategic recommendations to align internal systems with evolving standards.</p> </ul> <hr> <p><strong>Education & Experience – Required:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Bachelor’s degree in Electrical, Computer, or Systems Engineering.</p> <li> <p>15+ years of experience in RF communications systems and/or RF equipment development.</p> <li> <p>Demonstrated experience taking RF systems from concept through iterative design, specification development, and low-rate production.</p> <li> <p>Strong background in system architecture, requirements management, and performance assessment for communication systems.</p> </ul> <hr> <p><strong>Education & Experience – Assets:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Familiarity with DVB standards such as DVB-S2X and DVB-RCS2.</p> <li> <p>Solid understanding of digital communications, spread spectrum techniques, single and multi-carrier modulation (e.g., PSK, APSK, QAM).</p> <li> <p>Proficiency in MATLAB or equivalent tools for modeling and analyzing RF communication systems.</p> <li> <p>Deep knowledge of RF passive and active components and microwave frequency performance, including the effects of environmental factors such as rain fade.</p> <li> <p>Strong foundation in RF transceiver architecture and digital communication theory.</p> <li> <p>Excellent communication skills, with the ability to effectively engage stakeholders across engineering, management, and external partners.</p> <li> <p>Collaborative, adaptable, and capable of leading multidisciplinary teams in high-performance environments.</p> </ul> ]]>
</description>

<![CDATA[ As a RF Systems Engineer, you’ll be responsible for simulating and modeling the terrestrial and in-orbit communication systems for Lightspeed and support the definition of the architecture. <h2>Main Responsibilities</h2> <ul> <li>Simulate and model communication systems <li>Work with system architects, RF engineers, antenna engineers, User Terminal and Landing Station engineers, to partition functions between hardware and software domains <li>Model RF link performance and manage link budgets accounting for impairments through the different elements in the system <li>Derive specifications for RF links and RF and antenna subsystems <li>Characterize and analyze system performance. Develop and maintain performance budgets <li>Provide technical support to regulatory, coordination, and market access teams </ul> <h2>Education & Experience Required</h2> <ul> <li>Bachelor's degree in electrical engineering with emphasis in RF/microwave circuits or communication theory <li>At least 5 years of relevant experience RF communication systems <li>Knowledge of digital communication systems, spread spectrum, single and multi-carrier techniques, modulation types such as PSK, APSK, QAM <li>Specific experience with modulation standard such as DVB-S2X and DVB-RCS2, as well as with Adaptive Coding and Modulation (ACM) methods <li>Good experience in MATLAB or other tools for modeling and analyzing RF communication systems </ul> <h2>Specialized Knowledge, Skills & Abilities</h2> <ul> <li>Experience performing analysis and simulation of communication systems <li>Thorough understanding of RF passive and active components <li>Good understanding of active antenna beam forming technologies including digital beam forming, and fast beam hopping <li>Experience characterizing radio performance at microwave frequencies, including rain fade and its effects on the communication links <li>Knowledge of RF transceiver architectures and digital communication theor </ul> ]]>
